msg:Traveling to Hangzhou during the May Day holiday, I was afraid of being too congested and tired, so I chose this place as my base. I took a rest for one night and actually had an unexpected surprise. Room facilities: The size of this standard room is comparable to that of a high-end five-star hotel! Double basins, cloakroom, living space and bed are separated by a small partition. You can even call it an open-plan small suite. Value for money: 500 per night, including two breakfasts, my God! Breakfast: I am used to the sameness of international chain brands, and the breakfast here is another surprise. The Wenzhou glutinous rice is delicious, and there is freshly boiled porridge and freshly made salty soy milk. It is also good. I am full! Location and transportation: Next to the highway, the place is very friendly! Overall, it is good. If necessary, I will come again next time!
